padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1857053">thewho</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-14">11/14/24 22:39</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Bergamote 22 by Le Labo 3.75/5<br />
<br />
First impression is sharp bright lemon lime with a slice of synthetic notes. Almost like a sprite without carbonation. Wanted to love this since I love bergamote in fragrances. Bergamot usually doesn't last long and this isn't an exception. I wanted the other notes to start shining through to carry the perfume through a few hours. It is a bit similar to Guerlain's Bergamote Calabria but I think that one lasted a bit longer and wasn't as sharp in the beginning. There must be a note in here that doesn't jam with my nose. Don't get any of the vanilla or amber notes, which is a bit disappointing because that would be a very unique profile. Becomes a skin scent after 10 minutes and lasts a few hours.<br />
<br />
Free sample with purchase from Le Labo. Wore at home. Would not purchase a decant or full bottle.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="6327"comment_id="2349433"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Bergamote-22-6327.html?ccid=2349433#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2344163" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2330976" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Sniffing Jin"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2292211"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2292211.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Sniffing Jin" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2330976ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2330976" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.79); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2292211">Sniffing Jin</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-28">10/28/24 23:22</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Absolutely nothing ground breaking about this one, and personally find the whole house of Le Labo kind of mid.  BUT, dare I say this is one of the only accessible and decently performing bergamot dominating fragrances on the market. Yes, there are thousands of fragrances with bergamot but not many that that have scent profiles where the bergamot is the key player of 90% of the experience.<br />
<br />
Fell in love with Dior private line Cologne Royale, but it has since been discontinued and resells for around $500 on eBay which is obviously absurd.  Dior's cologne homme EDC is very similar but it lasts around an hour even with over spraying.  Jimmy Choo's Man Ice shares similar problems with performance despite being quite similar as well. Other fragrances in the same style have too many differences to my nose, so I settled with this one. Overall, straight bergamot with something woodsy and green in the base.  If bergamot is what you're looking for this is your best bet IMO.<br />
<br />
Pretty weak projection, overspray might be needed.  Gets me 5-6 hours on a good day.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="6327"comment_id="2330976"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Bergamote-22-6327.html?ccid=2330976#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.77); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1240871">Friedrich Wilhelm</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-12">09/12/24 17:53</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The king of versatility.<br />
<br />
The mix of bergamote, petitgrain, vetiver, and musk (and I get a LOT of musk from this), results in an incredibly fresh fragrance with plenty of masculinity.<br />
<br />
The musk also makes this smell a bit timeless, as it adds masculinity in the same way a fragrance like the original Acqua di Gio did. Many fresh fragrances today will use pepper or ambroxan to add a masculine element, but Bergamote 22 avoids both of them in favor of a more traditional approach. It works.<br />
<br />
As others have noted, the price can be a sore spot, but this is also very high quality and very wearable. If there could be such a thing as a fragrance worth $300 for 100ml, a fragrance that smells THIS good and can be worn literally anywhere might be it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; <br />
I'm certain there are better bergamot-forward smells for much less than this. Save your $300 and just imagine the smell xD</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="6327"comment_id="2229106"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Bergamote-22-6327.html?ccid=2229106#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2225186" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2225186" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="John C. Duboiz"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1777511"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1777511.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="John C. Duboiz" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2225186ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2225186" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1777511">John C. Duboiz</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-21">07/21/24 08:19</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Opens with a beautiful citrus. The top notes go in and out between Bergamot and Grapefruit. It also has hints of white floral notes, but not any specific flower.<br />
The mid takes a more musky turn as the citrus notes slowly fade away. It is a clean white musk, nothing animalic.<br />
In the mid, there also woody notes that start to appear, again not a clear woody note, but a cross between Cedar and Vetiver.<br />
In the dry down, you are left with a hint of citrus and even lesser white florals. Vetiver is the dominant note in the dry down, with musk playing second fiddle.<br />
<br />
Bergamote 22 is a very unique and artistic composition of a citrus perfume. Every note plays their part perfectly. It might remind you of some perfumes of the past due to how commonly some of the notes are used in perfumery (ex: bergamot, musk, vetiver) but the perfume itself is unique and beautiful enough to be worthy of your collection, especially if you are a lover of citrus.<br />
<br />
I will admit that the price was a hard pill to swallow, especially considering it's somewhat lackluster performance and longevity. But if you are a Fraghead (I am) then this is a masterpiece of a citrus that deserves your respect, so at the very least give it a try.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; <br />

<br />
However, I struggle with the price point a bit. It's a beautifully put together perfume but how innovative can you really be with this scent profile? There are so many equally gorgeous citrus scents for a fraction of the cost. I'm a lot more choosy when it comes to paying at this level. The scent must be so good I simply can't live without it in order to pay $500 for a FB. In this case I can find similar for 1/5 the price. Longevity not good enough. I may buy a full bottle but only once. <br />
<br />

Unlike Another 13, which I apparently have anosmia to, this scent is bold and only requires a few spritz for me and lasts a good while (6 hours). I wanted a good, solid citrus forward scent and I'm happy to have this in my collection. Truly unisex and unlike several other of their scents, this is ACTUALLY a Bergamot based scent. I'm looking forward to wearing this come summer. The only safe blind buy of Le Labo, imo. <br />
<br />
I thought Another 13 would be a safe blind but apparently there are several people, like me, who can't smell anything except the alcohol when it comes out. I'm so glad I paid $270 for a bottle of alcohol! Ok, that's not totally true. I get a little musk and ambrette but apparently my dad smells sweet flowers. The good thing is it works for a work scent since I work in a hospital, same with Bergamote since it's a green, clean, citrus scent. I can also layer Bergamote with Another and that works for me. Again, this actually has good longevity for a citrus scent and it truly leans neither feminine or masculine.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="6327"comment_id="2060612"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Bergamote-22-6327.html?ccid=2060612#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2059925" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Lime, bergamot, grapefruit.<br />
Juiciness doesn't last very long and the citrus makes way for some fresh, photorealistic, bitter, green petitgrain and neroli. These middle notes could lean slightly soapy to some.<br />
<br />
Dry, grassy vetiver underneath that has a ever-so-slightly 'curry-esque' character? The vetiver isn't overdone which is nice.<br />
<br />
VERDICT: For citrus enthusiasts. Very nice, fresh summer fragrance. Lavande in love by Bastide, or Citrus BatiKanga by Maison Crivelli are some good alternatives that won't require you getting a second mortgage.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; It‚Äôs got juuust enough musk and vanilla so that‚Äôs it‚Äôs comforting without compromising the freshness of the bergamot. The vetiver adds a nice touch too. It reminds me of wicker furniture warmed in the sun.<br />
<br />
Such an easy wear for all manner of occasions and probably the fragrance I reach for most.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="6327"comment_id="1986662"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Bergamote-22-6327.html?ccid=1986662#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1980591" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1925604" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="raldough"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1836605"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1836605.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="raldough" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1925604ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1925604" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1836605">raldough</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-09-11">09/11/23 17:05</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>scent: 8/10<br />
longevity: 6/10<br />
sillage: 6/10<br />
value: 3/10<br />
<br />
I first bought this for my birthday to bring and wear for a trip out to Honolulu thinking it would be the perfect setting for a fragrance like this. Such a bright and citrusy bergamot note opening, it's fresh, it's zesty, it's invigorating. This opening lasts up to 2-3 hours onto my skin and dries down to straight vetiver. It's not bad as it comes but much more simple if simple is your thing. <br />
<br />
I ended up selling the rest of my 50ml bottle at half volume because I thought the lack of projection and longevity could be due to the lack of chemistry my skin has with B22. <br />
<br />
A year later, I find myself revisiting this scent and it beams me back to when I was in Honolulu for vacation. Maybe it's the association of being on vacation on a lush tropical island but I forgot how good this scent was and maybe I just have yet to find a part of me being okay with skin scents.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; But 5 sprays of Bergamote 22 and you will enjoy a crispy, sparkling lime-green-citrus top (with a little jasmine), and an absolutely picture perfect finish of powdery vetiver, sweet vanilla, and the sharpness of cedar that will be with you a full 10+ hours. <br />
<br />
90% of the complaints below amount to "it's so good but it's expensive! üò†"</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="6327"comment_id="1886333"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Bergamote-22-6327.html?ccid=1886333#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1880249" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1059217">Beethoven&#039;s TeaParty</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-06-23">06/23/23 11:05</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Finally tried this and got a small decant. This is heavenly. Soft, sensual, clean and light. VERY unisex. I think this works on certain men, but to me, leans a bit more feminine. But still can work for either sex. Would smell divine on your wife or gf and would drive you crazy. <br />
<br />
Gallagher Bergamust smells almost exactly like this, except much more synthetic. While this is much more natural. Plus Bergamust has a sea salt or salty skin note that is pretty prevalent, where as this does not. Also, the notes of Bergamust smell sharp and raw and powerful, while in this, they smell understated, soft, clean, round and heavenly. I would also say D&amp;G Light Blue is in the same realm. Dior Cologne is a reach, but in the same vein, but is much more citrus forward and sharper than this. Versace Man Eau Fraiche is also in the same realm as this (musk/citrus). Not "the same", but similar. And that is MUCH cheaper, has much better projection, lasts longer. But it obviously isn't as soft and cozy and beautiful as this. <br />
<br />
This fragrance is kind of one dimensional though, all I get is a soft musk with the less forward Bergamot. And it stays that way the entire time. As everyone else has mentioned, the performance is a major disappointment and for the price is criminal! Lasts 3-6 hrs maybe and sits close to the skin the entire time. It cracks me up how many boutique or high end fragrances have SUCH poor performance, yet charge criminal prices for their product. And how cheaper fragrances have much better performance. It should be the exact opposite. <br />
<br />
But, I have to say, after all these years of wanting to try it, it totally lives up to the hype. Absolutely beeeeeautiful scent that is so clean, so soft, so cozy and surprisingly very sexy. If I could ever get my significant other to wear fragrances, and she same into a room wearing this, her clothes would be on the floor in 2 seconds flat with my lips on her neck ;)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/30910">AMajeedQT</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-05-14">05/14/23 17:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Straight-forward citrus floral.<br />
<br />
Fresh, citrusy bergamot dominate, supported by grapefruit, and softened by a touch of vetiver. The petitgrain and orange blossom and a soft white floral, lightly-jasminey touch. It has a light watery/aquatic nuance as well.<br />
<br />
Fresh, clean, citrusy, white floral, jasminey, and lightly aquatic.<br />
<br />
A comforting, bright, and beautiful scent. I like how round and not bitter B22 is, unlike many similar scents, that are usually neroli-centric. However, I am not paying $175 for 50ml of this rather common scent. Especially with its average performance. You are better off trying and getting something from the "reminds me of" section.<br />
<br />
Unisex, warm weather wear.<br />
<br />
"Like"</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="6327"comment_id="1833078"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Bergamote-22-6327.html?ccid=1833078#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1830467" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
It's a bitter, slightly sweet, citrus. The rind is up and about, but not pithy and bitter like biting into the wrong part of a grapefruit. It's fragrant and bright. The famous Le Labo musk is ever present, and Bergamote 22 just thrives on my skin. This is citrus heavy, and I ADORE citrus. The longevity is 9/10 for me, but it sits very close to the skin, so after about an hour (if it's more then I became anosmic) the longevity is like 4/10. Bottle is... I guess it's a 6/10 because I am infatuated with the idea of being to get refills for 20% off, but the bottle is boring. Sorry, it's minimalistic, not boring.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="6327"comment_id="1771391"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Bergamote-22-6327.html?ccid=1771391#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1764012" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Le Labo mixes their perfumes on the spot and they recommend you keep them in the refrigerator because they don't have preservatives so they spoil quicker. Initially, all my samples smelled out of this world. However, after a week or two, they lost their "magic" and settled into their actual smells. My reviews are based on what they will eventually smell like. <br />
<br />
Bergamote 22 is a very bright lemony scent with a unisex cedar drydown. It basically smells like those lemon household cleaning products, but in a good way. It's very bright, perfect for hot summer days. It may not be everyone's style but overall, a very pleasant smell. Unisex. <br />
<br />
Smell: 8 out of 10<br />
Longevity: 7 out of 10<br />
<br />

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1707269" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="McG1993"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/477821"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.477821.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="McG1993" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1707269ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1707269" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.74); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/477821">McG1993</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-12-11">12/11/22 17:05</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A fragrance is only worth however much you're willing to pay for it. With that being said, is Le Labo overpriced? I personally think it is and in as much as is possible, I try to stay away from overpriced fragrances. However, when it comes to Bergamote 22, it's kind of a different story. I think it's been a while since I've truly loved a fragrance as much as I love Bergamote 22. It's simple but it's bright, clean and very uplifting. Is it really worth its price tag? Perhaps not in the grand scheme of things but if you love it as much as I do, you might make an exception. In a world where so many prefer the scents of Dior's Sauvage, Prada's Luna Rossa, Ralph Lauren's Polo Blue, etc, Bergamote 22 means a whole lot more because it is everything I want it to be. It's not overpowering, intoxicating or complicated. The citrus is juicy and natural and the hints of green just make this smell like a beautiful, cozy day. This is not a heavy fragrance at all and projection and silliage is not impressive by any means. It lasts only 2 to 3 hours on my skin (best on the pulse points) and for the most part, this fragrance does stay close to the skin after its opening has left (I'm forgiving, though because most fragrances typically don't last much longer on my skin). Bergamote 22 may not be groundbreaking but it's simple, comforting and friendly.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="6327"comment_id="1707269"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Bergamote-22-6327.html?ccid=1707269#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1704854" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
Bergamote 22 definitely is what it says on the bottle, a hologram of bergamot starting of tart green bergamot juice and settling into a subtle earl grey vibe with some fresh linen like base notes, remaining green and refreshing throughout. <br />
<br />

Chanel Exclusifs Eau de Cologne is already a better deal and just as much vivid bergamot, subjectively a much nicer experience overall.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; I tried only 2, Bergamote 22 and Santal 33 where the clones were really better than the OG. Same like Armaf's Club de nuit sillage  vs  Creed's Silver mountain water but with no alcohol blast.<br />
<br />
Scent 7/10<br />
Longevity 4/10<br />
Sillage 6/10<br />
Value 2/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="6327"comment_id="1675120"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Bergamote-22-6327.html?ccid=1675120#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1662753" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
What I wanted Afternoon Swim to be like. Upon spraying it on skin, it opens with a lovely aroma of Bergamot EO, which compares favourably against my own EO of Bergamot. It sustains for about an hour before going into the woods with vetiver, cedar and musks. Reminiscent of Afternoon Swim, but more astringent and "neutral" smelling to my nose. <br />
<br />
It's more of a close-to-skin experience but leaves you wanting more after the magical opening fades away. <br />
<br />
I strongly suggest a sniff at it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="6327"comment_id="1601226"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Bergamote-22-6327.html?ccid=1601226#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1600639" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Like celery mushed with basil &amp; grapefruit rinds.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="6327"comment_id="1549078"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Bergamote-22-6327.html?ccid=1549078#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1547943" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1547943" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="VETTIVAER"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1436289"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="VETTIVAER" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1547943ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1547943" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1436289">VETTIVAER</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-04-21">04/21/22 10:36</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Bergamotte 22 is a supernaturally sparkling grapefruit experience. It is an abstract reconstruction of the bergamot odor using grapefruit, petitgrain and minuscule hints of vetiver and cedar. <br />
<br />
Grapefruit mercaptan (responsible for the sulphurous, sweaty odor in grapefruit peel) is ever so slightly detectable here, as is the raw, leafy, sappy bite of petitgrain. The sweaty grapefruit peel note is so faint, natural and familiar that I don't find it off-putting, but rather it adds charm, character and a sense of ease. <br />
<br />
 Cedar and invisible touches of vetiver lend the greens some backing. A very light touch of neroli connects the top notes to the base. A tremendous amount of effervescence is present in the opening. The faint, sluggish wafts of bergamot in the late drydown indicates the presence of synthetic musks. <br />
<br />
I cannot get this scent to last more than 3-4 hours, and even that is running on fumes. That is the only drawback, for the price of a bottle. <br />
<br />
It has been suggested to me that Jo Malone Grapefruit cologne can be layered with Basil and Neroli (for the same cost), and to my nose this is a fresher version of Le Labo's creation, minus the musks.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/300086">flyingfish</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-04-19">04/19/22 02:30</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It smells a little bit too "sweaty" for me. Lol. Like someone who's been sweating the whole day and doused themselves with a citrusy unisex perfume. Smells like CK2, which gives off the same vibe.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="6327"comment_id="1546295"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Bergamote-22-6327.html?ccid=1546295#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1544095" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1544095" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="The Wolf"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1263755"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1263755.gif" class="comments-avatar"alt="The Wolf" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Perris-Monte-Carlo/Oud-Imperial-Extrait-37829.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.37829.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Oud Imperial Extrait"title="Oud Imperial Extrait"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1544095ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1544095" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.86); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1263755">The Wolf</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-04-15">04/15/22 10:41</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I've smelled this many times and had decants but never bothered to write a review until I could get multiple proper wearings from a full bottle.  To me, this is the top bergamot scent you can buy along with Acqua Di Parma Bergamotto Di Calabria. I alternate between which is best, but I've decided they both hold the top spot. <br />
<br />
Performance here is better than the ADP.  Not to say that it's good because it's citrus, but it isn't abysmal like ADP. This has more sparkle and shine on the bergamot where ADP is more tart, tangy, and borderline sour. You'll need to put on 6 to 8 sprays to get 4 to 5 hours longevity. <br />
<br />
I liken this to an Italian Sports Car. üöò<br />
It's not practical, it's expensive, and it breaks down all the time. <br />
But, it's gorgeous, a blast to drive, and people love it.<br />
<br />
Whether or not it's worth the money is highly subjective. These are luxury products after all and nobody NEEDS them. But for me, the juice is worth the squeeze (to my wallet) and if you're a fan of bergamot, it doesn't get much better than this. <br />
<br />
Scent 10/10: a citrus masterpiece <br />
<br />
Performance 1.5/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="6327"comment_id="1544095"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Bergamote-22-6327.html?ccid=1544095#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1541825" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; The other question is the price. Why would I invest in something so expensive when I have to reapply constantly? It doesn‚Äôt make much sense (scents haha)‚Ä¶So, would I get a bottle of this? No, not at retail price. But if I found it at a heavy discount, then yes because I would not feel like I wasted my hard earned money/time on a fragrance that only lasts a couple of hours on my skin. If the longevity was better this would be a no brainer for me but at this price point unfortunately not.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="6327"comment_id="1525130"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Bergamote-22-6327.html?ccid=1525130#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1522981" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1350593">santeripe</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-03-14">03/14/22 09:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This doesn't even smell natural, this smells organic. So detailed, down-to-earth and beautifully put together. Aside from just bergamot, you also get some earthy touches in the opening that link it down to the base of light musk and slight sharpness from orange flower &amp; vetiver. This comes off like smelling an actual live flower, not just essential oil extracted from its petals. You get some "impuritites" too, but they're a part of the experience.<br />
<br />
FWIW, this definitely does not smell like CK One. It's one of my favorites, but its musky tea &amp; transparent citrus feel is totally different. This is more green, earthy, less "laundry-fresh" and way more complex. Performance is unfortunately pretty poor for the price. While expensive fragrances usually last longer than cheap ones, this is especially poor value for money, considering how many sprays you'll have to go through. Get a sample if you think your wallet can handle falling in love!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="6327"comment_id="1522981"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Bergamote-22-6327.html?ccid=1522981#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1520073" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I love bergamot, so there's nothing for me to complain about scent-wise. But I'm starting to realize that Le Labo doesn't have much staying power as a whole. That combined with the price has really soured my opinion of them as a brand. I feel like this is much more of a $30 - $50 brand, rather than $90 - $300.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="6327"comment_id="1476332"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Bergamote-22-6327.html?ccid=1476332#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1474954" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/990454">BlooBells</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-11-10">11/10/21 06:23</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A lot of the Le Labo fragrances are like gifts. Some are not well-wrapped, but most contain a lovely gift inside as long as you are patient (like Ylang 49, which is horrible on first spray, but a revelation after an hour) Bergamot 22 is not like that. It is a blast of joyful, zesty sunshine as soon as you spray it, and settles into a handsome and long lasting citrus orchestra with backing vocals from a type of restrained and clean vetiver. In my experience, citrus scents don‚Äôt usually have much longevity, so the people at Le Labo have done well with the formulation of this one. It is classy, upbeat and a good one for anyone who particularly enjoys neroli and citrusy frags with a herbal background.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="6327"comment_id="1443381"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Bergamote-22-6327.html?ccid=1443381#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1440007" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1312716">Glyph</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-11-04">11/04/21 10:22</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A very fine "clean white shirt fragrance," when you want to feel crisp and fresh. This has a note pyramid very much like Tom Ford's Grey Vetiver, although this has heavier concentrations of the bergamot and grapefruit at the top to make this juicier in feeling at the opening. The vetiver in this is also on the smokier side, which makes it a little (pleasingly) mysterious.  It also has a lovely long drydown where the cedar and vanilla take over.<br />
<br />
This engenders that elusive sense of having the wearer smell nice even though it's not entirely clear he or she is wearing perfume. You can see why this has been so popular in Manhattan, in the fashion industry in particular (I would expect the high price point adds to the mystique).</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; There have been a recent influx of Super Fakes<br />
(professionally crafted counterfeits) hitting secondary online marketplaces like Ebay and cosmetic websites.<br />
<br />
*Does your le labo atomizer mist? If so it is not real.*<br />
 <br />
This is one of the best pure bergamot frags in I've tried,  niche or otherwise. <br />
Tangy, Tart, green with a fantastic amber drydown.  Longevity is meh and by the time you get to the drydown it's a skin scent.  If money was no object,  this would be my signature citrus fragrance. <br />
But I'm using Bergamotto Di Calabria by Acqua di Parma and Commodity Bergamot which is very similar to Bergamote 22.<br />
<br />
I do love this fragrance, but I won't pay Le Labo prices for this.  For Santal33 and Noir however, I will pay the Le Labo premium.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="6327"comment_id="1388870"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Bergamote-22-6327.html?ccid=1388870#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1387078" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1238550">emerson10</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-05-18">05/18/20 10:46</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is my absolute favorite perfume forever. I have been collecting perfume forever. I've gone through phases. I've worn perfume for me and for others. Nothing compares. <br />
<br />
The Bergamot uplifts my mood, it's citrusy and fresh, yet WARM and well-rounded. This perfume tells a story. It's sweet, it's fresh, it's spicy. To me it's ozonic, it smells firey, but not like actually fire/smoke, if that makes sense.<br />
<br />
This is a perfect signature scent for someone who wants to smell sexy but not seductive, warm/kind but with an edge, approachable with mass appeal and yet totally unique. THE BEST. MOST AMAZING. SMELL. I wish I didn't love it so much because it's so expensive, but I do, and while I may not have electricity this month, I will smell electric.<br />
<br />
WHO I PICTURE THIS ON:<br />
me?!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="6327"comment_id="1177246"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Bergamote-22-6327.html?ccid=1177246#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1162014" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1162014" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="piyux"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1230413"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1230413.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="piyux" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Intense-2011-13016.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.13016.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Dior Homme Intense 2011"title="Dior Homme Intense 2011"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1162014ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1162014" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.78); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1230413">piyux</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-04-08">04/08/20 20:33</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Freshly squeezed lemons, is how this fragrance opens, it is all about the bergamot and its lemon/lime-like tones, very refreshing, very pleasant. But it is more than just a lemony scent, the woods, spices, musk, grapefruit, and vanilla can be detected a few moments after the initial opening. They help in creating a fantastic citrusy dominant fragrance. About 5 minutes into the dry-down the white flowers are noticeable, all tones achieve a more balanced level and the vanilla becomes more prominent adding a touch of sweetness. Clean and sharp, a fantastic refreshing fragrance.<br />
<br />
Category: Woody aromatic.<br />
Batch reviewed: 2020<br />
Wow Rating: 8/10. A clean, citrusy fragrance. Many fragrances feature citrus notes but this one does it very well, the quality is evident.<br />
Dislike Rating: 0/10: The fragrance contains no offensive notes.<br />
Uniqueness: 6/10. A good fresh fragrance but not unique in its area.<br />
Mass Appeal: 9/10. Very mass appeal, the fragrance will be well accepted and complimented.<br />
Projection: 4/10. Its projection is low.<br />
Sillage: 3/10. Sillage is also very low.<br />
Application: <br />
Longevity:  5/10. Five hours or less. Longevity is moderate but good for a citrus fragrance.<br />
Seasons: Spring, summer, and fall.<br />
Occasions: Any.<br />
Versatility: Very high, the fragrance is elegant, fresh, sporty, all in one.<br />
Gender: Unisex.<br />
Ages: Any.<br />
Recommendation: This may be the best bergamot based fragrance, quality, blending of notes. However, its price tag does not justify the product, consider other citrus fragrances instead.<br />
Blind-Buy: If you like citrus/lemon-based fragrances you can blind-buy this one.<br />
Similar: The market is full of citrusy fragrances. Here is a list of some of them, not necessarily the same as Bergamote 22, these add or take away some notes, but for the most part, they also contain bergamot as dominant note: Armaf Le Parfait Men Eau De Toilette By Armaf is a good one and affordable; Bond No 9 Bleecker Street By Bond contains citrus/bergamot notes but adds more green notes; Chanel Les Exclusifs ‚Äì Boy Eau De Parfum, add more floral notes; Creed Viking For Men Eau De Parfum By Creed adds more spices; Dua Fragrances ‚Äì Poseidon's Tux is a citrus-based fragrance; Dua Fragrances ‚Äì Caribbean Waters contains coconut and more gourmand notes; Dua Fragrances ‚Äì Lone Star is a citrus refreshing fragrance; Tom Ford Grey Vetiver Eau De Parfum By Tom Ford is very elegant citrus and vetiver fragrance. The most similar fragrance I can think of is Mancera Lemon Line, not identical but very similar and sweeter.<br />
Summary: Fresh, high quality, not the best projection but good for a citrus aromatic fragrance, highly versatile, this is a great fragrance for anyone.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1182402">MNadz</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-06-28">06/28/19 09:59</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>For all the great reviews I heard on this one, I was getting ready to be wowed.  So far from being amazed.<br />
<br />
Bergamot is OK, but I‚Äôve smelled juicier bergamot citrusy openings.  Dries down to earthy Vetiver, and I‚Äôve smelled better vetiver dry downs.  Is this OK...sure, but OK for this price is unacceptable.<br />
<br />
Longevity was average at best...4/5 hours on skin and clothes.  Performance is below average.<br />
<br />
I can not recommend this DNA, but try it out for yourself and get your own opinion.  Beauty of decants.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="6327"comment_id="1074089"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Bergamote-22-6327.html?ccid=1074089#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1183168" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
